                 <div class="cp-circle-control"></div> 
                 <div class="cp-controls"> <a class="cp-play" tabindex="1"><i class="glyphicon glyphicon-play"></i></a> <a class="cp-pause" style="display:none;" tabindex="1"><i class="glyphicon glyphicon-pause"></i></a> 
                 </div> 
                </div>
               </div>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="2303">人生</span>不是得到，就是学到。有些东西是你天生就有的，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1461">比如</span>长相，但有些则需要你通过学习去获得，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1461">比如</span>知识、能力、经验等等。后天学到比天生得到更为重要，只有通过自身的努力才能有最大的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2389">收获</span>。一个人，可以在失败中<span class="label-words" data-wid="2013">进步</span>，在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2013">进步</span>中<span class="label-words" data-wid="1545">成长</span>。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

              <div class="field-number">

               <div id="w33" class="audio circle-audio" data-ride="circleAudio" data-media="{&quot;mp3&quot;:&quot;http://f.hskcdn.com/old/web/13/34/220/audio/topic/8783.mp3&quot;}" data-extend="cp01994831">

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>　　一个花园里有一间小<span class="label-words" data-wid="2546">屋子</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2546">屋子</span>里住着花园的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2820">主人</span>，他是一个盲人。虽然他眼睛看不见，却把花园弄得非常漂亮，花园里总是开满了各种鲜花。</p> 
               <p>　　一位过路人惊奇地观赏着这漂亮的花园，不解地问盲人:“你这样做为的是什么呢？你<span class="label-words" data-wid="1795">根本</span>就看不见这些美丽的花呀。”</p> 
               <p>　　盲人笑了，说:“我可以告诉你四个<span class="label-words" data-wid="2092">理由</span>:第一，我喜欢园艺工作，第二，我可以抚<span class="label-words" data-wid="2172">摸</span>我的花，第三，我可以<span class="label-words" data-wid="2540">闻</span>到它们的香味，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2797">至于</span>第四个<span class="label-words" data-wid="2092">理由</span>，则是因为你。”</p> 
               <p>　　“我？但是，你<span class="label-words" data-wid="1795">根本</span>不认识我啊。”路人说。</p> 
               <p>　　“是的，我不认识你，但是我知道有一些像你一样的人，会在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2177">某</span>个时间从这儿经过，这些人会因为看到我美丽的花园而心情愉快，而我也因此能有机会和你在这儿谈这件事。”</p>
              </div>
             </div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="2433">所谓</span>“好钢用在刀刃上”，就是要把<span class="label-words" data-wid="2017">精力</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1927">集中</span>在最出成绩的地方。只要你细心总结一下，就会发现:你得到的百分之八十的帮助<span class="label-words" data-wid="2072">来自</span>于你百分之二十的朋友，而你投入的百分之八十的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2017">精力</span>却只得到百分之二十的收入。我们常常把大多数时间和<span class="label-words" data-wid="2017">精力</span>花在并不很重要的地方。一个年轻的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2598">小伙子</span>卖<span class="label-words" data-wid="1448">保险</span>时，头一个月仅挣了一千元。他仔细<span class="label-words" data-wid="1742">分析</span>了他的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2596">销售</span>图表，发现他百分之八十的收入<span class="label-words" data-wid="2072">来自</span>百分之二十的客户，但是他却对所有的客户花费了同样的时间。于是，他把<span class="label-words" data-wid="2017">精力</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1927">集中</span>到最有希望的客户上。不久，他一个月赚了六千元。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">

                 <div class="field-audio">
                  <div id="w38" class="audio circle-audio" data-ride="circleAudio" data-media="{&quot;mp3&quot;:&quot;http://f.hskcdn.com/old/web/13/34/220/audio/topic/8788.mp3&quot;}" data-extend="cp01994831">
                   <div id="w38-jplayer" class="cp-jplayer"></div>

                     <div class="cp-buffer-1"></div>

             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ1 - Đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">39-41</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               39-41
              </div> 
              <div class="field-audio">
               <div id="w41" class="audio circle-audio" data-ride="circleAudio" data-media="{&quot;mp3&quot;:&quot;http://f.hskcdn.com/old/web/13/34/220/audio/topic/8791.mp3&quot;}" data-extend="cp01994831">
                <div id="w41-jplayer" class="cp-jplayer"></div> 
                <div id="w41-container" class="cp-container"> 
                 <div class="cp-buffer-holder"> 
                  <div class="cp-buffer-1"></div> 
                  <div class="cp-buffer-2"></div> 
                 </div> 
                 <div class="cp-progress-holder"> 
                  <div class="cp-progress-1"></div> 
                  <div class="cp-progress-2"></div> 
                 </div> 
                 <div class="cp-circle-control"></div> 
                 <div class="cp-controls"> <a class="cp-play" tabindex="1"><i class="glyphicon glyphicon-play"></i></a> <a class="cp-pause" style="display:none;" tabindex="1"><i class="glyphicon glyphicon-pause"></i></a> 
                 </div> 
                </div>
               </div>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>　　我的一位朋友多次获得乒乓球单打<span class="label-words" data-wid="1834">冠军</span>。有乒乓球爱好者向他请教成功的秘诀，出人意料，他竟然说“成功之前先要做好失败的准备”。在进入正式比赛前，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2385">事先</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1552">承认</span>不论怎样做，你不可<span class="label-words" data-wid="1467">避免</span>会出现这样那样的失误，做好这样的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2418">思想</span>准备就可以减少<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>压力，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1599">从而</span>取得比赛的成功。他还举例说，在一次全国乒乓球大赛中，他和另一位著名的乒乓球运动员争夺冠亚军，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>确实厉害，一上场就先赢了他两局，但由于他在进场前就做好了失败的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>准备，所以没有慌乱，完全放开来打，挺住了，最后反倒是他战胜了<span class="label-words" data-wid="1694">对手</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　成功之前先做好失败的准备，并非放弃对成功的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2839">追求</span>，而是让我们<span class="label-words" data-wid="1731">放松</span>心情，放下包袱，轻装上阵，如此一来反倒容易成功。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               42-43
              </div> 
              <div class="field-audio">
               <div id="w45" class="audio circle-audio" data-ride="circleAudio" data-media="{&quot;mp3&quot;:&quot;http://f.hskcdn.com/old/web/13/34/220/audio/topic/8795.mp3&quot;}" data-extend="cp01994831">
                <div id="w45-jplayer" class="cp-jplayer"></div> 
                <div id="w45-container" class="cp-container"> 
                 <div class="cp-buffer-holder"> 
                  <div class="cp-buffer-1"></div> 
                  <div class="cp-buffer-2"></div> 
                 </div> 
                 <div class="cp-progress-holder"> 
                  <div class="cp-progress-1"></div> 
                  <div class="cp-progress-2"></div> 
                 </div> 
                 <div class="cp-circle-control"></div> 
                 <div class="cp-controls"> <a class="cp-play" tabindex="1"><i class="glyphicon glyphicon-play"></i></a> <a class="cp-pause" style="display:none;" tabindex="1"><i class="glyphicon glyphicon-pause"></i></a> 
                 </div> 
                </div>
               </div>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>　　“好的”“一定会有办法的”“没问题”，每天都能说出这种积极话语的人，他们的每一天也都会过得非常顺利，即使遇到了困难。相反，每天<span class="label-words" data-wid="2295">嚷</span>着“太<span class="label-words" data-wid="2740">糟糕</span>了”“太让人<span class="label-words" data-wid="1745">愤怒</span>了”“太讨厌了”“真<span class="label-words" data-wid="1645">倒霉</span>”的人，遇到的困难也<span class="label-words" data-wid="1786">格外</span>多，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2731">运气</span>也<span class="label-words" data-wid="2568">显得</span>极其<span class="label-words" data-wid="2740">糟糕</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　语言就好像<span class="label-words" data-wid="1784">鸽子</span>的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1562">翅膀</span>，只有<span class="label-words" data-wid="2010">尽力</span>扇动，才能飞到理想的彼<span class="label-words" data-wid="1432">岸</span>。积极<span class="label-words" data-wid="2083">乐观</span>的语言，能带给我们美好、快乐的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2303">人生</span>。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">
              <div class="field-children">
               <div class="exercise-view exercise-child exercise-xzt" data-eid="8796" data-lid="92" data-sid="89" data-pid="8795" data-tid="122">
                <div class="field-heading">
                 <div class="field-number">
                  42
                 </div> 
                 <div class="field-question ans-hide">
                  <p>每天都说“没问题”的人会怎样？</p>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　有时候，你被人误解了，你不想解释，所以选择沉默。本来就不是所有的人都得了解你，因此你<span class="child-number">46</span>对全世界解释。也有时候，你被最爱的人误解，难过到不想解释，也只有选择沉默。全世界的人都可以不懂你，但他应该懂。如果连他都不能懂你，还有什么话可说？生活中总有无法解决的问题，<span class="child-number">47</span>不是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2431">所</span>有的对错都能讲清楚，甚至可能<span class="child-number">48</span>就没有真正的对与错。那么，不想说话，就不说吧。在多说也没有什么帮助的情况下，也许沉默就是最好的解释。</p>
              </div>

           <div class="item">
            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="8984" data-lid="92" data-sid="92" data-pid="0" data-tid="127">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ1 - Chọn từ điền vào chỗ trống trong đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">49-52</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               49-52
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　<span class="label-words" data-wid="1600">从前</span>，有个聪明人的马被偷走了。他知道是谁偷的，就去向那个人要马，但那人拒绝归还，一口咬定说:“这是我的马。”</p> 
               <p>　　聪明人用双手遮住了马的双眼，对那个偷马人说:“<span class="child-number">49</span>这马真是你的，你一定知道马的哪只眼睛是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2563">瞎</span>的。”</p> 
               <p>　　“右眼。”偷马人<span class="child-number">50</span>地说。</p> 
               <p>　　聪明人放下蒙右眼的手，马的右眼并没有<span class="label-words" data-wid="2563">瞎</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　“我记错了，<span class="child-number">51</span>。”偷马人<span class="label-words" data-wid="1925">急忙</span>辩解道。</p> 
               <p>　　聪明人又放下蒙左眼的手，马的左眼也没有<span class="label-words" data-wid="2563">瞎</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　“我又说错了……”偷马人还想狡辩。</p> 
               <p>　　“不错，你是错了。这<span class="label-words" data-wid="1564">充分</span>说明马不是你的。”聪明人说完就<span class="child-number">52</span>着马回家了。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">
              <div class="field-children">
               <div class="exercise-view exercise-child exercise-xzt" data-eid="8985" data-lid="92" data-sid="92" data-pid="8984" data-tid="127">

               <p>　　文化就像一个<span class="label-words" data-wid="2531">胃</span>，如果健康的话，各种<span class="label-words" data-wid="2379">食物</span>都能接受，都能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2593">消化</span>，并<span class="label-words" data-wid="2832">转变</span>成自己身体所需要的各种<span class="child-number">57</span>。这个<span class="label-words" data-wid="2531">胃</span>如果这也不能吃，那也不适应，那是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2531">胃</span>自己出了<span class="child-number">58</span>。为了<span class="label-words" data-wid="2531">胃</span>好，就需要它能够接受自已原来不适应的各种<span class="label-words" data-wid="2379">食物</span>，而不是只让它吃它喜欢的那几样。同样，<span class="child-number">59</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1692">对待</span>其他文化最好的办法不是拒绝而是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2555">吸收</span>。一个能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2555">吸收</span>不同文化的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2531">胃</span>才是健康的、有活力的，并且最终会把其他文化<span class="child-number">60</span>到自己的文化中去。</p>

               <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>学家对颜色与人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2276">情绪</span>之间的关系进行了研究。一般情况下，红色表示<span class="label-words" data-wid="2083">乐观</span>、热情，能使人<span class="label-words" data-wid="2276">情绪</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2298">热烈</span>、饱满；黄色表示快乐、明亮，能使人<span class="label-words" data-wid="1565">充满</span>喜悦之情；绿色表示<span class="label-words" data-wid="1876">和平</span>，能使人的心里有<span class="label-words" data-wid="2231">平静</span>之感。不同颜色会给人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2276">情绪</span>带来不同影响，使人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>活动发生变化。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

              <div class="field-subject text-indent">
               <p>在<span class="label-words" data-wid="1815">古代</span>，“疾”与“病”的意思不同。“疾”是指不易觉察的小病，如果不及时<span class="label-words" data-wid="1507">采取</span>有效<span class="label-words" data-wid="1610">措施</span>，就会发展到<span class="label-words" data-wid="2054">可见</span>的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1556">程度</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1540">称</span>为“病”。这种非病非健康的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>，世界卫生组织称为“第三<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>”，中国叫做“亚健康<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>”。处于亚健康<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>的人，容易感到<span class="label-words" data-wid="2217">疲劳</span>，适应能力也会下降。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">

                </div>
               </div> 
               <div class="field-option-wrap" data-no="1">

              <div class="field-number">
               71-74
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　大家一定都坐过出租车。<span class="label-words" data-wid="1947">假如</span>，我们再坐一次出租车，做一个<span class="label-words" data-wid="2377">实验</span>:上车后，你先不要讲话。司机如果问你“去哪里”，你就说“你自己看着办吧”。你信不信，即使是开了几十年出租车的老司机，这个时候也没有办法把车开走。为什么？因为司机只知道怎样选择最佳路线把你送到你想去的地方。他知道方法、手段和技巧，并且把它做好。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2797">至于</span>你想去的地方，司机并不知道，只有你知道你想去的地方。所以，如果连你都不知道你想去哪里，司机当然就不知道往哪里开。生活中的这个小故事告诉人们一个<span class="label-words" data-wid="1922">基本</span>哲理:目的，永远在技巧和方法前面。一个人如果一开始就不知道他的目的地在哪里，他就永远到不了他想去的地方。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

           <div class="item">
            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="9305" data-lid="92" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="24">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ1 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">75-78</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               75-78
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　“我发现你这个人很不<span class="label-words" data-wid="2080">老实</span>。”女友小丽盯着我的眼睛。</p> 
               <p>　　“我……”我一下子不知道说什么好，“我怎么了我？ ”</p> 
               <p>　　“你的手机给我用用。”女友<span class="label-words" data-wid="2346">伸</span>手要我的手机。我<span class="label-words" data-wid="1773">赶快</span>把手机<span class="label-words" data-wid="1666">递</span>了过去。</p> 
               <p>　　女友把我的手机放在桌子上，用家里的座机打了一个电话，然后按下免提键:“喂，文哥吗？我是小丽。”文哥是我一个特别要好的朋友，我们俩从小关系就特铁。</p> 
               <p>　　文哥:“你好你好！有什么事情啊？”</p> 
               <p>　　小丽:“文哥，我有点儿急事找李洋，他和你在一起吗？”</p> 
               <p>　　文哥:“在一起呢。我俩正商量点儿事情。你等一下，他在<span class="label-words" data-wid="1519">厕所</span>呢，我给你叫去。李洋，小丽找你……哎呀，小丽，他还在<span class="label-words" data-wid="1519">厕所</span>呢。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2657">要不</span>等他出来，我让他给你打回去？”</p> 
               <p>　　小丽:“好的，谢谢文哥。”</p> 
               <p>　　一<span class="label-words" data-wid="1656">滴</span>冷汗从我的头上慢慢地往下流……</p> 
               <p>　　15<span class="label-words" data-wid="2160">秒</span>钟后，放在桌子上的手机突然响起来，我的第二<span class="label-words" data-wid="1656">滴</span>冷汗也开始往下流。小丽得意地看着我，按下了接听键。</p> 
               <p>　　“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2627">幸亏</span>你小子开机了，你在哪儿呢？小丽刚给我打电话找你呢。不过哥们儿替你<span class="label-words" data-wid="1637">挡</span>住了，说你小子正在我们家<span class="label-words" data-wid="1519">厕所</span>呢。怎么样，够意思吧？你呀，快点儿给小丽打电话，别忘了说你在我这儿……”</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">
              <div class="field-children">
               <div class="exercise-view exercise-child exercise-xzt" data-eid="9306" data-lid="92" data-sid="96" data-pid="9305" data-tid="24">

                  75
                 </div>

                  <p>文中“关系特铁”的意思最可能是：</p>
                 </div>
                </div> 
                <div class="field-body">
                 <div class="field-items cols-2">
                  <div class="field-option-wrap" data-no="0">
                   <div class="field-option">
                    <span class="field-no">A</span>
                    <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="1526">产生</span>了<span class="label-words" data-wid="2140">矛盾</span></p>
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                  <div class="field-option-wrap" data-no="1">
                   <div class="field-option">
                    <span class="field-no">B</span>
                    <p>从小就认识</p>
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                  <div class="field-option-wrap answer" data-no="2">

                    <p>关系有所<span class="label-words" data-wid="1763">改善</span></p>

              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ1 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn

             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               79-82
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　有一天，两只饥饿的小熊<span class="label-words" data-wid="1957">捡</span>到了一大块儿面包。哥哥说:“应该由我来分，因为我是哥哥。”弟弟说应该由我来分，因为我年龄小，妈妈常说你得让着我。” 后来，它们各抓住一边，把面每包掰开了。结果却是一块儿大，一块儿小。这时，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2631">兄弟</span>俩又发生了争执，都想要较大的一块儿。这时，一只同样饥饿的狐狸恰好经过这里。两只小熊<span class="label-words" data-wid="2073">拦</span>住狐狸，想让狐狸<span class="label-words" data-wid="2818">主持</span>公道，帮它们分一分这块儿面包。狐狸高兴得<span class="label-words" data-wid="1490">不得了</span>。它二话没说，抓起那块儿较大的面包就<span class="label-words" data-wid="2656">咬</span>了一大口。结果，原来大块儿的面包变成了小块儿的，小块儿的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1719">反而</span>成了大的。两只小熊还是不满意。狐狸对它们说:“别看急，别着急。”它又抓起较大块儿的面包<span class="label-words" data-wid="2656">咬</span>了一口，结果还是一块儿大一块儿小。两只小熊还是不满意，狐狸又抓起较大块儿的面包<span class="label-words" data-wid="2656">咬</span>了一口……最后，两只小熊都只得到一小口儿看起来一样大小的面包屑。</p>
              </div>

           <div class="item">
            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="9315" data-lid="92" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="24">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ1 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">83-86</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               83-86
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　他从小就有个理想，那就是长大后成为作家。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2849">自从</span>有了这个理想之后，他每天都坚持写作。每次写完之后，他都会拿着自己的文章看了又看，改了又改，然后<span class="label-words" data-wid="1565">充满</span>希望地寄往各地的报社、杂志社。可<span class="label-words" data-wid="2675">遗憾</span>的是，他虽然写了那么多文章，而且自己也觉得写得不错，伯乐却<span class="label-words" data-wid="2381">始终</span>没有出现过——所有的报社、杂志社都从未<span class="label-words" data-wid="1703">发表</span>过他的文章，甚至连一封<span class="label-words" data-wid="2496">退</span>稿信都没有给他寄过。这让他既难过又心寒。</p> 
               <p>　　很多年后的一天，他终于收到了他投稿最多的那家报社的一封信。当他欣喜若狂地打开时，却发现那不过是封<span class="label-words" data-wid="2496">退</span>稿信。被泼了一<span class="label-words" data-wid="2211">盆</span>冷水之后，深感<span class="label-words" data-wid="1908">灰心</span>的他打算放弃了。稍稍清醒一些后，他发现那封信中有一个给他的小<span class="label-words" data-wid="1963">建议</span>:“你每次寄来的稿子我都看过，这么多年来你<span class="label-words" data-wid="2381">始终</span>如一地投稿，由此可以看出你是一个很努力的青年。但我不得不<span class="label-words" data-wid="2675">遗憾</span>地告诉你，你将很难在写作方面有所<span class="label-words" data-wid="1548">成就</span>。不过，不知道你有没有注意到，你的钢笔字写得越来越好。所以我觉得，如果你向书法方面发展，可能会更好，也比较容易成功……”这几句话引起了他的深思。最后，虽然他<span class="label-words" data-wid="2671">依然</span>热爱写作，但还是决定放弃写作，改向钢笔书法进军。</p> 
               <p>　　这个人叫张文举，现在是中国非常著名的硬笔书法家。他的故事告诉人们，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2303">人生</span>当中的许多失败，往往是由于人们尚未找到最适合自己的路而<span class="label-words" data-wid="1640">导致</span>的。那么，在适当的时候让理想转个弯儿，也许会收到意想不到的效果。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">

                 <div class="field-question">
                  <p>他为什么放弃了写作？</p>

           <div class="item">
            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="9320" data-lid="92" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="24">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ1 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">87-90</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               87-90
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　职场幸福指数，是工作<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>和质量的直接反映。一<span class="label-words" data-wid="2585">项</span>对1560名职业女性的调查<span class="label-words" data-wid="2570">显示</span>，46.2%的被调查者在工作中一点儿幸福感也没有，工作压力太大、不能兼顾工作和<span class="label-words" data-wid="1940">家庭</span>成为影响职场幸福指数的重要<span class="label-words" data-wid="2688">因素</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　对工作的满意度，是职场幸福指数的最直接的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2465">体现</span>。调查<span class="label-words" data-wid="2570">显示</span>，66.9%的女性对日前的工作不满意，表示“很满意”者仅占6.1%。谈到职场不幸福的原因，大家认为工作压力太大、不能兼顾<span class="label-words" data-wid="1940">家庭</span>、<span class="label-words" data-wid="2634">休闲</span>时间太少是主要原因，发展<span class="label-words" data-wid="2063">空间</span>小、工资太低、人际关系不好等也是影响幸福感的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2688">因素</span>。其中，37.6%的被调查者表示，因为工作太紧张，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1922">基本</span>没<span class="label-words" data-wid="2017">精力</span>顾及<span class="label-words" data-wid="1940">家庭</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　调查<span class="label-words" data-wid="2570">显示</span>，随着年龄增大，女性的职场幸福感有所提高，36岁以上的女性对工作满意者占两成，能从工作中获取幸福感者占76%。随着年龄的增长，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1940">家庭</span>对女性<span class="label-words" data-wid="2017">精力</span>的牵涉会<span class="label-words" data-wid="2579">相对</span>减少，经济压力也有所降低，工作不再仅仅是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2773">挣钱</span>的工具。经过磨练，这些人的心态也更好，职场幸福感自然会增强。</p> 
               <p>　　谈到对<span class="label-words" data-wid="2181">目前</span>工作最不满意的地方，39.1%的被调查者认为<span class="label-words" data-wid="2634">休闲</span>时间太少，发展<span class="label-words" data-wid="2063">空间</span>小、工资太低<span class="label-words" data-wid="1738">分别</span>占20.3%和20%。随着工作节奏的加快和生活水平的提高，女性对<span class="label-words" data-wid="2634">休闲</span>时间的渴望更强。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2634">休闲</span>和<span class="label-words" data-wid="1731">放松</span>有助于提高职场幸福指数，这一点应引起用人<span class="label-words" data-wid="1630">单位</span>的注意。</p>
              </div>

        var paperDate = new Date(), stopOffsetDate, timeLeft = 7200, timeTotal = 7200;
        paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + 7200);
        $('#paper-countdown').on('click', '.btn[data-op]', function () {
            var op = $(this).data('op');
            if(op === 'start' && stopOffsetDate){
                paperDate = new Date();
                paperDate.setHours(paperDate.getHours() + stopOffsetDate.hours);
                paperDate.setMinutes(paperDate.getMinutes() + stopOffsetDate.minutes);
                paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + stopOffsetDate.seconds);
                $('#paper-countdown').countdown('setFinalDate', paperDate);
            }
            $('#paper-countdown').countdown(op).find('.btn[data-op]').toggleClass('hide');
            $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('resetTime');
        }).countdown(paperDate, function (event) {
            timeLeft = event.offset.hours * 60 * 60 + event.offset.minutes * 60 + event.offset.seconds;
            $('.cd-time', this).html(event.strftime('%H:%M:%S'));
        }).on('stoped.countdown', function (event) {
            stopOffsetDate = event.offset;
        });
        $('#exercise-list').on('slid.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            var $el = $(e.relatedTarget), index = $el.index();
            $('#exr-prev').prop('disabled', $el.prev().length === 0);
            if ($el.next().length > 0) {
                $('#exr-next').removeClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').addClass('hide');
            } else {
                $('#exr-next').addClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').removeClass('hide');
            }
            if (!$el.data('autoPlayed')) {
                $el.find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
                $el.data('autoPlayed', 1);
            } else if (e.direction === 'left') {
                $el.prev().stopPlay();
            } else {
                $el.next().stopPlay();
            }
            $(this).exerciseTest('setSubmitParams', 'recent_index', index);
            activeAnswerSheetPanel(index);
        }).on('slide.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            $('.item.active .exercise-view', this).trigger('next.hsk.test');
        }).on('beforeSubmit', function (e) {
            e.submitParams.duration = timeTotal - timeLeft;
        });
        $('#exr-submit').on('click', function (e) {
            if(window.confirm('确定要提交试卷吗?')){
                $('.item.active > .exercise-view', '#exercise-list').trigger('next.hsk.test');
                $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('submit', true).done(function (data) {
                    window.location.href = '/vi/5/4/report?pid=' + data.exam_id;
                });
            }
        });
        function activeAnswerSheetPanel(index) {
            var $collapse = $('li[data-slide-to=' + index + ']', '#answer-sheets').closest('.collapse');
            if (!$collapse.hasClass('in')) {
                $collapse.prev('.panel-heading').find('[data-toggle=collapse]').trigger('click');
            }
        }
        activeAnswerSheetPanel(0);
        window.setTimeout(function () {
            $('.item.active', '#exercise-list').data('autoPlayed', 1).find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
        }, 1000);

jQuery('#emw-34fcb4d5').on('show.bs.modal', function(event){
    if(event.relatedTarget){
        var el = $(event.relatedTarget), url = el.attr('href') || el.data('url'), frm = $('iframe', this), 
        self = $(this), e = $.Event('beforeLoading.wm', {relatedTarget: el, url: url, loadingUrl : url});
        self.trigger(e);
        if(frm.data('_url') !== e.url){
            var title = el.data('title') || el.attr('title');
            title && $('.modal-title', this).html(title);
            frm.attr('src', e.loadingUrl).data('_url', e.url).parent().addClass('loading');
            self.trigger('afterLoading.wm', e.loadingUrl);
        }
    }
}).find('iframe').on('load', function() {
    $(this).height($(this.contentDocument).height()).parent().removeClass('loading');
});
